<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">9)100 % of the paid-in share capital of the company Alcon Nederland B.V., with a par value of CHF&#160;28,424;</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">10)99 % of the paid-in share capital of the company Alcon Italia S.p.A., with a par value of CHF&#160;2,198,746;</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">11)100 % of the paid-in share capital of the company Alcon Norge AS, with a par value of CHF&#160;9,790;</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">12)100 % of the paid-in share capital of the company Alcon Polska Sp. z.o.o., with a par value of CHF&#160;300,000;</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">13)90 % of the paid-in share capital of the company Alcon Portugal Produtos e Equipamentos Oftalmologicos, Lda., with a par value of CHF&#160;35,100;</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">14)100 % of the paid-in share capital of the company Alcon Sverige AB, with a par value of CHF&#160;18,190;</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">15)100 % of the paid-in share capital of the company Alcon Pharmaceuticals Ltd., with a par value of</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">CHF&#160;100,000;</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">16)100 % of the paid-in share capital of the company Alcon S.A., with a par value of CHF&#160;100,000;</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">17)100 % of the paid-in share capital of the company Alcon Laboratuvarlari Ticaret AS, with a par value of CHF&#160;1,420,000;</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">18)100 % of the paid-in share capital of the company Alcon Laboratories (South Africa) (Pty) Ltd., with a par value of CHF&#160;58,528;</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">19)100 % of the paid-in share capital of the company Alcon Korea Ltd., with a par value of CHF&#160;200,000;</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">20)100 % of the paid-in share capital of the company Alcon Hong Kong Limited, with a par value of CHF&#160;14,122;</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">21)98 % of the paid-in share capital of the company Alcon Japan Ltd., with a par value of CHF&#160;9,525,120;</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">22)100 % of the paid-in share capital of the company Alcon Laboratories (Philippines), Inc., with a par value of CHF&#160;651,124;</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">23)100 % of the paid-in share capital of the company Alcon Pte Ltd., with a par value of CHF&#160;143,533;</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">24)30 % of the paid-in share capital of the company Alcon Laboratories (Thailand) Ltd, with a par value of CHF&#160;10,050;</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">25)100 % of the paid-in share capital of the company Alcon Laboratories (Australia) Pty. Ltd., with a par value of CHF&#160;2,397,000;</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">26)100 % of the paid-in share capital of the company Alcon Canada Inc., no par value;</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">27)100 % of the paid-in share capital of the company Alcon (Puerto Rico) Inc., with a par value of CHF&#160;142;</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">28)100 % of the paid-in share capital of the company Alcon Laboratories, Inc., with a par value of CHF&#160;7,100;</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">29)100 % of the paid-in share capital of the company AlconLab Ecuador S.A., with a par value of CHF&#160;18,000;</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">30)industrial and intellectual property.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">These contributions are received at a total value of CHF&#160;298,022,970. In consideration for such contribution in kind, the Company allots to Nestl&#233; Ltd, Cham and Vevey, 50,000 fully paid re&#173;gistered shares of the Company with a total nominal value of CHF&#160;50,000,000. The Company enters into its books CHF&#160;50,000,000 as
share capital and CHF&#160;248,022,970 as reserves.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div></td></tr><tr>
<td valign="top" width="10%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></td>
<td align="left" valign="top" width="4%">
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">2</font></div></td>
<td align="left" valign="top" width="46%">
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Aus Anlass der Kapitalerh&#246;hung der Gesellschaft von CHF&#160;54'000'000 auf CHF&#160;60'000'000, leistet die Nestl&#233; AG, Cham und Vevey, die folgenden Einlagen:</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">1)ein Darlehen an Alcon Laboratories Inc. von CHF&#160;306'400'000,</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">2)ein Darlehen an Alcon Laboratoires (UK) Ltd. von CHF&#160;16'585'200,</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">3)ein Darlehen an Laboratoires Alcon S.A. von CHF&#160;37'240'200.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Diese Einlagen werden zu einem Wert von insgesamt CHF&#160;360'225'400 &#252;ber&#173;nommen. Als Gegenleistung f&#252;r diese Sacheinlage gibt die Gesellschaft der Nestl&#233; AG, Cham und Vevey, 6'000 voll einbezahlte Namen&#173;aktien der Gesellschaft mit einem Nominalwert von ins&#173;ge&#173;samt CHF&#160;6'000'000 aus. Dabei werden bei der
Gesellschaft CHF&#160;6'000'000 als Aktienkapital und CHF&#160;354'225'400 in die Reserven gebucht.</font></div></td>
<td valign="top" width="10%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></td>
<td align="left" valign="top" width="4%">
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">2</font></div></td>
<td align="left" valign="top" width="46%">
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">In connection with the increase of the Company's share capital from CHF&#160;54,000,000 to CHF&#160;60,000,000, Nestl&#233; Ltd, Cham and Vevey, effects the following contributions:</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">1)a loan to Alcon Laboratories Inc. of CHF&#160;306,400,000,</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">2)a loan to Alcon Laboratoires (UK) Ltd. of CHF&#160;16,585,200,</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">3)a loan to Laboratoires Alcon S.A. of CHF&#160;37,240,200.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">These contributions are received at a total value of CHF&#160;360,225,400. In consideration for such contribution in kind, the Company allots to Nestl&#233; Ltd, Cham and Vevey, 6,000 fully paid re&#173;gistered shares of the Company with a total nominal value of CHF&#160;6,000,000. The Company enters into its books CHF&#160;6,000,000 as share
capital and CHF&#160;354,225,400 as reserves.</font></div></td></tr><tr>
<td valign="top" width="10%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></td>
<td valign="top" width="4%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></td>
<td valign="top" width="46%">

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Verbindlicher Originaltext</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Original Language</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Falls sich zwischen der deutschen und einer anderen sprachlichen Fassung dieser Statuten Differenzen ergeben, gilt der deutsche Originaltext.</font></div></td>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">In the event of deviations between the German version of these Articles of Incorporation and any version in another language, the German authentic text prevails.</font></div></td></tr></table></div>
